<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сирота.html>сирота́</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sirotá</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ский</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-skij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиротский.html>сиро́тский</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sirótskij</span>) (<i>no comparative</i>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> orphan; orphan's
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сиротский.html>сиро́тская</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sirótskaja</b> žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>orphan's</b> life</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> poor, miserable</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relational<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> orphan care
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сиротский.html>сиро́тский</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дом.html>дом</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sirótskij</b> dom</i> ― <span class="e-translation">orphanage</span> (literally, “<span class="e-literally"><b>orphan-care</b> house</span>”)</div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сирый.html>си́рый</a> (24633)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сиръ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sirŭ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">сирꙑи</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">siryi</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sirъ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">antiquated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> orphaned, lonely, deserted</li></ol>

***систематизировать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:систематизировать.html>систематизи́ровать</a> (25873)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">systematisieren</i> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-овать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; see also <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***систематический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:систематический.html>системати́ческий</a> (15624)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perhaps from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">systematisch</i> + <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:систематический.html>системати́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sistematíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>systematic, methodical</li>
<li>regular
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:систематический.html>системати́ческие</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:пропуск.html>про́пуски</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:занятие.html>заня́тий</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sistematíčeskije</b> própuski zanjátij</i> ― <span class="e-translation">regular absence from classes</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сиська.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сиська.html>си́ська</a> (20287)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиська.html>си́ська</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sísʹka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиська.html>си́ськи</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиська.html>си́ськи</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиська.html>си́сек</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">си́сечка</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> boob
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>Её</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сиська.html>си́ськи</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бы́ли</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:огромный.html>огро́мными</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:мягкий.html>мя́гкими</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:подушка.html>поду́шки</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:из.html>из</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:плоть.html>пло́ти</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Jejó <b>sísʹki</b> býli ogrómnymi i mjáxkimi, kak podúški iz plóti.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Her boobs were huge and soft, like fleshy pillows.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***сиять.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сиять.html>сия́ть</a> (2431)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*sijati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сиять.html>сия́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">sijátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to shine, to beam</li>
<li><i>(facial expression)</i> to shine, to beam, to be radiant
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сиять.html>сия́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:от.html>от́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:радость.html>ра́дости</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>sijátʹ</b> ot rádosti</i> ― <span class="e-translation">shine with joy</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to shine, to be resplendent</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a> (28)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Perfective form of archaic Russian <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:казать.html>каза́ть</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">kazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*kazati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skazátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:говорить.html>говори́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to say, to tell
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2007</b>,  “<span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>скажи́</a></span>”, performed by <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">Сплин</span> (Splean):</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Cyrl e-quotation" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>скажи́</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:что.html>что</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:любить.html>люблю́</a><br /> <a href = vnd.unilang:без.html>Без</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>неё</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:весь.html>вся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:равный.html>равна́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ноль.html>нулю́</a></span><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Skaží</b>, što ja jejó ljubljú<br /> Bez nejó vsja žiznʹ ravná nuljú</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Tell</b> her that I love her<br /> Without her all life amounts to nothing</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказаться.html>сказа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skazátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказываться.html>ска́зываться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to affect <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоедание.html>недоеда́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сказаться.html>сказа́лось</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nedojedánije <b>skazálosʹ</b> na zdoróvʹje.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Malnutrition affected (his/her) health.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to manifest itself <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to show (some effect)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pretend to be (by reporting)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">светла́на <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сказаться.html>сказа́лась</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришла́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:совещание.html>совеща́ние</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svetlána <b>skazálasʹ</b> bolʹnój i ne prišlá na soveščánije.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Svetlana pretended to be sick and didn't come to the meeting.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зка</a> (2080)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skazátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ка</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-ka</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зка</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skázka</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зки</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказка.html>ска́зок</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">literary genre</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> tale; fairy tale</li>
<li>lies, fabrication</li></ol>

***сказываться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказываться.html>ска́зываться</a> (8678)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказывать.html>ска́зывать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skázyvatʹ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to tell, to say <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">poetic</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказываться.html>ска́зываться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skázyvatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сказаться.html>сказа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to affect <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">na</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:недоедание.html>недоеда́ние</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сказываться.html>ска́зывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:здоровье.html>здоро́вье</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Nedojedánije <b>skázyvajetsja</b> na zdoróvʹje.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Malnutrition is affecting (his/her) health.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to manifest itself <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">v</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> in</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>, to show (some effect)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to pretend to be (by reporting)
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru">светла́на <a href = vnd.unilang:часто.html>ча́сто</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:сказываться.html>ска́зывается</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:больной.html>больно́й</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Svetlána částo <b>skázyvajetsja</b> bolʹnój.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Svetlana often pretends to be sick.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***скак.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скак.html>скак</a> (24661)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Deverbal from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скакать.html>скака́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">skakátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скак.html>скак</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skak</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скак.html>ска́ка</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скак.html>ска́ки</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скак.html>ска́ков</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gallop</li></ol>

***скакать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:скакать.html>скака́ть</a> (4607)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Slavic">Proto-Slavic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="sla-pro">*skakati</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скакать.html>скака́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">skakátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:проскакать.html>проскака́ть</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:скакнуть.html>скакну́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to ride (on) a horse</li>
<li>to hop, to jump (about)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">ride on a horse</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ездить.html>е́здить</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:верх.html>верхо́м</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">jézditʹ verxóm</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">jump</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыгать.html>пры́гать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">prýgatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
